00299.xml
 OPTIONAL TAG: use only if revising EAD-encoded finding aid.
<revisiondesc>
<change>
<date>Date of change</date>
<item>Updated because of ?</item>
</change>
</revisiondesc>

 OPTIONAL TAG: use to spell out usage restrictions. 
<userestrict>
<head>Usage Restrictions</head>
<p></p></userestrict>

 OPTIONAL TAG: use if MICROFILM is available. Filmed date(s) can be a span, a single year, or a month and year. Do not tag with <unitdate>. If there's only one reel, call it Reel 1 and list contents (could be "Entire collection"). If there are multiple reels, repeat <item> tags for each reel.
<altformavail encodinganalog="530">
<head>Alternate Form of Material</head>
<p>Microfilm copy (filmed [give date(s) if known; if not, delete this part]) available.
<list type="simple">
<item>Reel 1: [contents, e.g., Folders 1-14]</item>
</list></p>
</altformavail>

 OPTIONAL TAG: use if alternate form of material OTHER THAN MICROFILM is available.
<altformavail encodinganalog="530">
<head>Alternate Form of Material</head>
<p>[What it is].</p>
</altformavail>

 OPTIONAL TAG: use if there are additional guides (card files, dealer or donor lists, old finding aids, etc.).
<otherfindaid>
<head>Additional Descriptive Resources</head>
<p>[What they are]></p>
</otherfindaid>

ALKMS228.xml
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME 
type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. 
To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
Enter ENCODINGANALOG value of 5450_ for biog. or 5451_ for historical note, or use 
<head> element

unique number for the collection, e.g. VAA1234. Put this full identifier both in the identifier 
attribute and in the value of the eadid element.

date.  The stylesheets will supply a comma where appropriate.

 value of @findaidstatus should be 'originaldraft', 'inprogressdraft', 'editinprogress', or 'editedfulldraft' 
 This is a description of the electronic finding aid, not the original finding aid or the collection 
 Make title "xxxx mss., yyyy-yyyy"
Make subtitle "Papers, yyyy-yyyy, of [person] at the Lilly Library, Indiana University, Bloomington, Indiana
description of how the finding aid was created, for example: XML finding aid derived from
[paper by means of scanning and OCR] [OCR file edited for typographical errors before encoding]
[typescript by rekeying] [word processing program and version number]
[<extref href=""  title="" actuate="onrequest" show="new">HTML collection description</extref>]. 
 iso three-digit 639-2 value for @langcode can be found at http://www.loc.gov/standards/iso639-2/langcodes.html 
 revisiondesc is required 
 record when the finding aid is initiated in first 'change' element, with subsequent changes listed below the first, and the final 'change' element indicating date finding aid completed 
 the 'frontmatter' element is a wrapper that bundles prefatory text found before the start of the archival description <archdesc>. It focuses on the creation, publication, or use of the finding aid rather than information
about the materials being described. Examples include a title page, preface, dedication, and instructions for
using a finding aid. 
 information should be included as you would wish it to appear on a titlepage of a printed finding aid 
it is possible to include graphics using extptr 
 @type value may alternatively be 'bulk' 
 use the label attribute for these elements to determine what label is displayed 
 if both linear feet and number of items included, separate by lb tag 
 element organization deprecated in DTD version 2002; @encodinganalog may be used to differentiate between 351 subfield a (organization) and subfield b (arrangement). 
 required for collection level; optional for lower levels 
 required; 'descgrp' element replaces admininfo element in 2002 DTD 
 required, if appropriate 
 recommended; this information would be included for marc amc record 
 should include all personal and corporate names, and subject headings 
 unittitle is the only required element within component 
 possible values for @level include: class, collection, file, fonds, item, otherlevel, recordgrp, series, subfonds, subgrp, subseries

 revisiondesc is required 
 record when the finding aid is initiated in first 'change' element, with subsequent changes listed below the first, and the final 'change' element indicating date finding aid completed 
 the 'frontmatter' element is a wrapper that bundles prefatory text found before the start of the archival description <archdesc>. It focuses on the creation, publication, or use of the finding aid rather than information
about the materials being described. Examples include a title page, preface, dedication, and instructions for
using a finding aid. 
 information should be included as you would wish it to appear on a titlepage of a printed finding aid 
it is possible to include graphics using extptr 
 @type value may alternatively be 'bulk' 
 use the label attribute for these elements to determine what label is displayed 
 record the name of the repository even if its display is to be suppressed 
 do not include separating punctuation between the unit title and the unit date - the stylesheets will supply a comma where appropriate. 
 unitdate may be repeated if both bulk and inclusive dates are recorded 
 record the type of date - bulk or inclusive - in the type attribute. 
 recommended 
 if both linear feet and number of items included, separate by lb tag 
 langmaterial element replaces langmaterial attribute on eadheader element in 2002 DTD 
 if collection includes significant non-english material add code to langmaterial element 
 required; 'descgrp' element replaces admininfo element in 2002 DTD 
 required even if unrestricted 
 recommended for manuscript collections, if known 
 required even if unrestricted 
 required, can be short 
 required for collection level; optional for lower levels 
optional

NTDIJC001.xml
Template updated 20080408 by J. Allison-Bunnell
Remember to name and save documents using the OCLC code + local filename. Documents that are revised/updated after initial submission much be submitted with precisely the same filename.
The following section is header information that describes the finding aid
To link to your logo, click on the diamond in the <extptr> tag below and enter the full
URL of the digital logo file in the HREF attribute. Describe image in TITLE attribute, eg., University of 
Oregon logo
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME 
type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. 
To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
Enter ENCODINGANALOG value of 5450_ for biog. or 5451_ for historical note, or use 
<head> element
A finding aid without a series or container list may end here.
Be sure to choose the appropriate TYPE attribute for this collection
At each <c0x> level, be certain that you have chosen the appropriate LEVEL attribute!

To link to your logo, click on the diamond in the <extptr> tag below and enter the fullURL of the digital logo file in the HREF attribute. Describe image in TITLE attribute, eg., University of Oregon logo
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
Enter ENCODINGANALOG value of 5450_ for biog. or 5451_ for historical note, or use <head> element

PriestRapidsDamOpeningPHColl802.xml
 Describe UW's original; LABEL attribute of <physdesc> should  be "original"
 Describe UW's original; LABEL attribute of <physdesc> should  be "original"
 Describe UW's original; LABEL attribute of <physdesc> should  be "original"
If an image is provided as illustration, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags: identifying info about the image, repository info, and UW  negative number using the format: 
Food court, Seattle World's Fair, 1962. Special Collections, UW Libraries, UW19577z   
No info needed in <resource> element.
In <daoloc>, enter into the HREF attribute the full URL of the image file. 
Eg. http://www.lib.washington.edu/specialcoll/images/ead/M3783.jpg. Also enter MIME type of digital file 
(eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute, eg. Image 
of food court, Seattle World's Fair, 1962.
In <bioghist> below, see ENCODINGANALOG attribute; enter "5450_" for biography or "5451_" for 
organization history
HISTORICAL BACKGROUND NOTE
Also add one or more browsing terms from the NWDA term list at 
http://nwda.wsulibs.wsu.edu/BrowsingTermsAlphaJan302006.pdf
For a one-title collection, intellectual content is described above in <archdesc>. Below, in <c01>, 
describe primarily physical aspects of/restrictions on each generation (version) of the title as applicable; 
use a separate <c01> for each version. If segments are described, use <c02> in the viewing copy and add 
timecode, segment-level scope/content info, etc.
 Describe UW's original; LABEL attribute of <physdesc> should  be "original"
 Describe viewing copy/print if applicable; LABEL attribute of <physdesc> should  
contain "viewing"

TrumanWashingtonStatePatrolFilmPHColl825.xml
If a visual collection contains no associated text, enter in <langmaterial> below "No textual 
or other language materials are included in the collection." Otherwise give language info as in default 
text below.
If an image is provided as illustration, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags: identifying info about the image, repository info, and UW  negative number using the format: 
Joe Smith, 1938. Special Collections, UW Libraries, UW19577z   No info needed in <resource> element.
In <daoloc>, enter into the HREF attribute the full URL of the image file. 
Eg,  http://www.lib.washington.edu/specialcoll/images/ead/MS3783.jpg. Also enter MIME type of digital file 
(eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute, eg. Image of Mike 
Lowry, 1982.
In <bioghist> below, see ENCODINGANALOG attribute; enter "5450_" for biography or "5451_" for 
organization history
HISTORICAL BACKGROUND NOTE
Also add at least one browsing term from the NWDA browsing term list at 
http://nwda.wsulibs.wsu.edu/BrowsingTermsAlphaJan302006.pdf
Use the c01 section to state the name of a series if applicable. For subseries, files, or items, use c02's 
and/or C03's and C04's (depending on how coll. is arranged). Each time you need to state the name of a new 
top-level series, insert a new c01. For an item-level-only inventory (no series), use only c01, level="item."

VincentLeonStuartPHColl822.xml
If an image may be associated with the finding aid, use the following <daodesc> and <daoloc>
elements. In <daodesc>, enter descriptive info inside <p> tags: identifying info about the image, 
repository info, and moving image number using the format: 
Tyree Scott with airport official, Seattle-Tacoma airport, 1969. Special Collections, UW Libraries, VHS 11
In <daoloc>, enter into the "href" attribute the full URL of the image file. 
Eg,  http://www.lib.washington.edu/specialcoll/images/ead/MS3783.jpg.
In <bioghist> below, see "encodinganalog" attribute; enter "5450_" for biography or "5451_" for 
organization history
HISTORICAL BACKGROUND NOTE
Also add one or more browsing terms from the NWDA term list at 
http://nwda.wsulibs.wsu.edu/nwdabrowsinglist.htm
Use the c01 section to state the name of a series if applicable. For subseries or items, use c02's and/or 
C03's, then close c01. Each time you need to state the name of a new top-level series/subgroup, 
click Insert menu, Element, and select c01. For an item-level-only inventory (no series), use only c01, level="item."

WUGGU_3.xml
Template updated 20080408 by J. Allison-Bunnell
Remember to name and save documents using the OCLC code + local filename. Documents that are revised/updated after initial submission much be submitted with precisely the same filename.
The following section is header information that describes the finding aid
To link to your logo, click on the diamond in the <extptr> tag below and enter the full
URL of the digital logo file in the HREF attribute. Describe image in TITLE attribute, eg., University of 
Oregon logo
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME 
type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. 
To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
A finding aid without a series or container list may end here.
Be sure to choose the appropriate TYPE attribute for this collection
At each <c0x> level, be certain that you have chosen the appropriate LEVEL attribute!

WaSMAR0200_01.xml
The following section is header information that describes the finding aid
To link to your logo, click on the diamond in the <extptr> tag below and enter the full
URL of the digital logo file in the HREF attribute. Describe image in TITLE attribute, eg., University of 
Oregon logo
Use corpname element for creator of organizational records.  (For personal or family creators, use 
persname or famname elements.)  Add/verify information in SOURCE, RULES, ROLE, and ENCODINGANALOG 
attributes.  Look up name of organization in Library of Congress Name Authority File (http://authorities.loc.gov).  If it 
appears, use that form of the name and set SOURCE="lcnaf".  If an authorized form of the name does not appear, 
formulate according to DACS or AACR2 and set RULES attribute to "dacs" or "aacr2" as appropriate.
Set ROLE="creator" (you may also use "collector" if appropriate) and ENCODINGANALOG="110"
for corpname and "100" for persname).
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME 
type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. 
To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
Enter ENCODINGANALOG value of 5450_ for biog. or 5451_ for historical note, or use 
<head> element
Preferred format for citing the collection: samples follow.  Choose photos or records, then fill in collection
title and record series number for the collection.  Delete the other sample.
Search for personal, corporate, and family name headings in the 
	 Library of Congress Authorities (http://authorities.loc.gov) or other source.  If 
	 source is LC Authorities, set SOURCE attribute to "lcnaf"; if from another authority, 
	 use the appropriate code. If no authorized name exists, create a name according to 
	 DACS or AACR2.  Leaving SOURCE blank, fill in RULES attribute with "dacs" or "aacr2" 
	 as appropriate.  In ENCODINGANALOG, use 6XX for names as subjects (600=personal, 
	 610=corporate) and 7XX for names as creators (700=personal, 710=corporate).  In ROLE, 
	 use "creator" for creators and "subject" for subjects.
Place name; if established in LCSH or other authority, use SOURCE="lcsh" or 
		  code for other authority.  ENCODINGANALOG="651" and ROLE="subject".
Subject term; indicate source of term in SOURCE attribute, such as 
	 "lcsh" or "lctgm"; see Best Practices Guidelines for further details. If you cannot find appropriate terms in LCSH, 
you may use terms from the City Clerk's Thesaurus and enter "local" under SOURCE.
NWDA browsing terms; at least one is required.  SOURCE="nwda", ALTRENDER="nodisplay", 
and ENCODINGANALOG="690"

Search for personal, corporate, and family name headings in the 
	 Library of Congress Authorities (http://authorities.loc.gov) or other source.  If 
	 source is LC Authorities, set SOURCE attribute to "lcnaf"; if from another authority, 
	 use the appropriate code. If no authorized name exists, create a name according to 
	 DACS or AACR2.  Leaving SOURCE blank, fill in RULES attribute with "dacs" or "aacr2" 
	 as appropriate.  In ENCODINGANALOG, use 6XX for names as subjects (600=personal, 
	 610=corporate) and 7XX for names as creators (700=personal, 710=corporate).  In ROLE, 
	 use "creator" for creators and "subject" for subjects.
Place name; if established in LCSH or other authority, use SOURCE="lcsh" or 
		  code for other authority.  ENCODINGANALOG="651" and ROLE="subject".
Subject term; indicate source of term in SOURCE attribute, such as 
	 "lcsh" or "lctgm"; see Best Practices Guidelines for further details. If you cannot find appropriate terms in LCSH, 
you may use terms from the City Clerk's Thesaurus and enter "local" under SOURCE.
NWDA browsing terms; at least one is required.  SOURCE="nwda", ALTRENDER="nodisplay", 
and ENCODINGANALOG="690"

If a visual collection contains no associated text, enter in <langmaterial> below "No textual 
or other language materials are included in the collection." Otherwise give language info as in default 
text below.
If an image is provided as illustration, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags: identifying info about the image, repository info, and UW  negative number using the format: 
Joe Smith, 1938. Special Collections, UW Libraries, UW19577z   No info needed in <resource> element.
In <daoloc>, enter into the HREF attribute the full URL of the image file. 
Eg,  http://www.lib.washington.edu/specialcoll/images/ead/MS3783.jpg. Also enter MIME type of digital file 
(eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute, eg. Image of Mike 
Lowry, 1982.
In <bioghist> below, see ENCODINGANALOG attribute; enter "5450_" for biography or "5451_" for 
organization history

Also add at least one browsing term from the NWDA browsing term list at 
http://nwda.wsulibs.wsu.edu/BrowsingTermsAlphaJan302006.pdf

         <head>Related Material</head>
         <p>## (MARC 544 1)</p><p>&scrc_name; has made a concerted effort over the 
years to ensure that its manuscript and rare books holdings complement each other.  
As a result, many of our manuscript collections are supported by books, pamphlets, 
serials and other items which are cataloged in the Rare Books Collection.  Please be 
sure to search &summitref; for these related materials.</p>
      </relatedmaterial>

<c01 level="series"><did><unittitle>##</unittitle></did>
               <Permissible values for @TYPE for first CONTAINER are 'Box' 'Oversize' 'Volume' 'Carton' or 'Map-Case'.>
               <Permissible values for @TYPE for second CONTAINER are 'Folder' 'Frame' 'Page'  or 'Reel'.>
            <c02 level="subseries"><did><unittitle>##</unittitle><unitdate normal="##" type="inclusive">##</unitdate><container type="Box">1</container></did></c02>
         </c01>

NOTE TO PROCESSOR: There will be two validation errors the first time you open
            this file. 1. Revise archdesc level="n". 2. Either delete scopecontent or add a
            paragraph.
====== OPTIONAL TAG: use only if revising EAD-encoded finding aid.
               Delete section if you are not revising the finding aid. =======

ohrc041.xml
 The value of eadid should follow the pattern of archive or library code, and then a 
            unique number for the collection, e.g. InU-ohrc003. Put this full identifier both in the identifier attribute and in the value of the eadid element. 
 This is a description of the electronic finding aid, not the 
                original finding aid or the collection 
 Change date to date of first publication, change rights statement if other entity claims rights over the finding aid (not the collection)
 revisiondesc is required 
 record when the finding aid is completed in first change element, 
            with subsequent changes
            listed below the first 
 The TYPE attribute can be used to categorize the finding aid as an inventory, register, or other format. 
 per RLG guidelines recommendation, do not nest unitdate element within
                unittitle element 
 Do not include the type="inclusive" attribute if it is a single date 
 do not include separating punctuation between the unit title and the unit
                date.  The stylesheets will supply a comma where appropriate. 
 if collection includes signinficant non-english material add code to
                langmaterial element 
 If no abstract is provided, use part of scopecontent note 
 required even if unrestricted 
 required 
 unittitle is the only required element within component 
 possible values for @level include: class, collection, file, fonds, item,
                otherlevel, recordgrp, series, subfonds, subgrp, subseries

ohs1999001.xml
The following section is header information that describes the finding aid
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME 
type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. 
To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
Enter ENCODINGANALOG value of 5450_ for biog. or 5451_ for historical note, or use 
<head> element

 If you have an index which is not related to a specific series (e.g. a list of exhibitions) provide a link to the <odd> (where the index will be encoded) here e.g.  

<note><p><ref target="index1">See index for List of Selected Correspondents from Series #.</ref></p></note>  

If you have more than one index of this kind change the index target number accordingly e.g. <ref target="index2">.

 use this format if you have series only, no subseries

<note><p><ref target="seriesindex1">See index for List of Selected Correspondents from Series 1.</ref></p></note>

<odd encodinganalog="500" id="seriesindex1">
<head>[Title of Index]</head>
<p></p>
</odd>

vintroux_k.xml
 TEMPLATE VERSION 1.11, 17 Oct 2008
Revised standard blurb for related material 
All items are required unless marked OPT.  Any optional items 
not used should be commented out so that they don't appear in the viewable
 document.
Enter revisions in the format "## date - ## change (## initials)"
Use archref, not extref, to link to related collections.
<separatedmaterial encodinganalog="544 0">
         <head>Separated Material</head>
         <p>## OPT (MARC 544 0)</p>
      </separatedmaterial>
<otherfindaid encodinganalog="555">
         <head>Other Related Finding Aids</head>
         <p>## OPT (MARC 555)</p>
      </otherfindaid>
For each, include source if possible (aat, lcsh, local, etc). Some have 
defaults set in the template.
<appraisal encodinganalog="583">
         <head>Appraisal Information</head>
         <p>## OPT (MARC 583)</p>
      </appraisal>
<accruals encodinganalog="584">
         <head>Accruals</head>
         <p>## OPT (MARC 584)</p>
      </accruals>

warservicebureau.xml

wasmhi1953_345.xml
The following section is header information that describes the finding aid
To link to your logo, click on the diamond in the <extptr> tag below and enter the full
URL of the digital logo file in the HREF attribute. Describe image in TITLE attribute, eg., University of 
Oregon logo
To link to an image from the collection, use the following elements. In <daodesc>, enter caption info 
inside <p> tags. In <daoloc>, enter full URL of the digital image file in HREF attribute;  enter MIME 
type of digital file (eg., "image/jpeg") in ROLE attribute; enter brief description of image in TITLE attribute. 
To link to a logo, use <extptr> or <extref> inside <publisher> in <eadheader> instead.
